Zill/N00487_MVSF
Zillow Home Value Index (Neighborhoods): Median Value Per Sq. Ft. (All Homes) - Wynwood - Edgewater, Miami
The Zillow Home Value Index is Zillow's estimate of the median market value of all homes within the neighborhood of Wynwood - Edgewater, Miami. This number is derived by taking the estimated home value for each home and dividing it by the homes square footage. This data is calculated by Zillow Real Estate Research (www.zillow.com/research) using their database of 110 million homes.
